***domineren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:domineren.html>domineren</a> (17053)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:domineren.html>domineren</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">dominer</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:domineren.html>domineren</a></strong>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:domineren.html>domineren</a></b>

***donder.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:donder.html>donder</a> (1689)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">donre</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:donner.html>donner</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:donder.html>donder</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thunar</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thonar</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þunraz</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)tenh₂-</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:donner.html>Donner</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">tonger</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">thunder</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:donder.html>donder</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>thunder <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">sound produced by a thunderstorm</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:donderdag.html>donderdag</a> (2506)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">donresdach</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">donredach</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thonaresdag</i>, from late <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*Þunras dagaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">day of <a href = vnd.unilang:thor.html>Thor</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Dunnersdag</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Donnerstag</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">tongersdei</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">Thursday</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">torsdag</i>.

***donderen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:donderen.html>donderen</a> (32705)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">donren</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:donderen.html>donderen</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:donder.html>donder</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:donderen.html>donderen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to thunder
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">In <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verte.html>verte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoor.html>hoor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:donderen.html>donderen</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I can hear it <b>thunder</b> in the distance.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make a thunderous sound, especially with one's voice
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">'<a href = vnd.unilang:hou.html>Hou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mee.html>mee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a>!', <b><a href = vnd.unilang:donderde.html>donderde</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">'<a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>Stop</a> that right now!', <b>thundered</b> the <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to plummet, tumble
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leerling.html>leerling</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verloor.html>verloor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:evenwicht.html>evenwicht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:donderde.html>donderde</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:achterover.html>achterover</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stoel.html>stoel</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The pupil <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>lost</a> his balance and <b>tumbled</b> backwards off his chair.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***donk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:donk.html>donk</a> (54672)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">donc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:dunk.html>dunk</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">dung</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">in placenames</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*dungz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰengʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cover; covering</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Possibly related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:donker.html>donker</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dark</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:donk.html>donk</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:donk.html>donken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:donk.html>donkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:sandy.html>sandy</a> hill, typically of glacial origin, protruding above a silty area.
<ul><li><b>2009</b>, Marjolein <a href = vnd.unilang:kerkhof.html>Kerkhof</a>, <i>Pijnacker-Nootdorp. <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:archeologische.html>archeologische</a> verwachtings- <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> beleidsadvieskaart</i>, in <i>Delfste <a href = vnd.unilang:archeologische.html>Archeologische</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rapporten.html>Rapporten</a> 96</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:erfgoed.html>Erfgoed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:delft.html>Delft</a>/Sidestone Press (publ.), page 48.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">donst</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dons.html>dons</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Down, small bird <a href = vnd.unilang:feathers.html>feathers</a> used as insulation material in <a href = vnd.unilang:covers.html>covers</a> and sleeping <a href = vnd.unilang:bags.html>bags</a>.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dons.html>dons</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:donzen.html>donzen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dons.html>donsje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a> cover (e.g. a duvet) filled with down.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly diminutive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A piece of down or fluff.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a> cover</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">donsdeken</span></li></ul>

***dood.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dood.html>dood</a> (137)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dôot</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:doet.html>doet</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">dōt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*daud</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*daudaz</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">dead</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">dead</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">død</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dood.html>dood</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doder.html>doder</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">doodst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dead</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/East_Flanders" class="extiw" title="w:East Flanders">East</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Flanders" class="extiw" title="w:West Flanders">West Flanders</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A lot.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_3">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dôot</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:doet.html>doet</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">dōth</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">dōt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*dauþu</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*dauþuz</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">dead</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:tod.html>Tod</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">death</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">død</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***doodgraver.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:doodgraver.html>doodgraver</a> (30607)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dootgravere</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dood.html>dood</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:graver.html>graver</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***doodleuk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:doodleuk.html>doodleuk</a> (45617)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dood.html>dood</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leuk.html>leuk</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doodleuk.html>doodleuk</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>cold-bloodedly, <a href = vnd.unilang:flat.html>flat</a> out, calmly, coolly; in an unconcerned way; without showing care; heartlessly
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">doodgemoederd</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">brutaalweg</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijskoud.html>ijskoud</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>in a tongue in cheek or phlegmatic way; with a deadpan delivery</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doodleuk.html>doodleuk</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:flat.html>flat</a> out, simple, straightforward</li>
<li>terribly funny</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:doof.html>doof</a> (2959)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dôof</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">dōf</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*daubaz</i>.

<ol><li>deaf</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doven.html>doven</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to extinguish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pot.html>pot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:pot.html>pot</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doofpot.html>doofpot</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doofpot.html>doofpotten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doofpot.html>doofpotje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>an old-fashioned metal canister with a tight <a href = vnd.unilang:lid.html>lid</a>, in which remaining coals and other fuel <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> put to <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> down.</li>
